A scheme is the\\n34: // foundation for a versioned API and versioned configuration over time.\\n35: //\\n36: // In a Scheme, a Type is a particular Go struct, a Version is a point-in-time\\n37: // identifier for a particular representation of that Type (typically backwards\\n38: // compatible), a Kind is the unique name for that Type within the Version, and a\\n39: // Group identifies a set of Versions, Kinds, and Types that evolve over time. An\\n40: // Unversioned Type is one that is not yet formally bound to a type and is promised\\n41: // to be backwards compatible (effectively a \\\"v1\\\" of a Type that does not expect\\n42: // to break in the future).\\n43: //\\n44: // Schemes are not expected to change at runtime and are only threadsafe after\\n45: // registration is complete.\\n46: type Scheme struct {\\n47: \\t// gvkToType allows one to figure out the go type of an object with\\n48: \\t// the given version and name.\\n49: \\tgvkToType map[schema.GroupVersionKind]reflect.Type\\n50: \\n51: \\t// typeToGVK allows one to find metadata for a given go object.\\n52: \\t// The reflect.Type we index by should *not* be a pointer.\\n53: \\ttypeToGVK map[reflect.Type][]schema.GroupVersionKind\\n54: \\n55: \\t// unversionedTypes are transformed without conversion in ConvertToVersion.\\n56: \\tunversionedTypes map[reflect.Type]schema.GroupVersionKind\\n57: \\n58: \\t// unversionedKinds are the names of kinds that can be created in the context of any group\\n59: \\t// or version\\n60: \\t// TODO: resolve the status of unversioned types.\\n61: \\tunversionedKinds map[string]reflect.Type\\n62: \\n63: \\t// Map from version and resource to the corresponding func to convert\\n64: \\t// resource field labels in that version to internal version.\\n65: \\tfieldLabelConversionFuncs map[schema.GroupVersionKind]FieldLabelConversionFunc\\n66: \\n67: \\t// defaulterFuncs is a map to funcs to be called with an object to provide defaulting\\n68: \\t// the provided object must be a pointer.\\n69: \\tdefaulterFuncs map[reflect.Type]func(interface{})\\n70: \\n71: \\t// converter stores all registered conversion functions. It also has\\n72: \\t// default converting behavior.\\n73: \\tconverter *conversion.Converter\\n74: \\n75: \\t// versionPriority is a map of groups to ordered lists of versions for those groups indicating the\\n76: \\t// default priorities of these versions as registered in the scheme\\n77: \\tversionPriority map[string][]string\\n78: \\n79: \\t// observedVersions keeps track of the order we've seen versions during type registration\\n80: \\tobservedVersions []schema.GroupVersion\\n81: \\n82: \\t// schemeName is the name of this scheme.  If you don't specify a name, the stack of the NewScheme caller will be used.\\n83: \\t// This is useful for error reporting to indicate the origin of the scheme.\\n84: \\tschemeName string\\n85: }\\n86: \\n87: // FieldLabelConversionFunc converts a field selector to internal representation.\\n88: type FieldLabelConversionFunc func(label, value string) (internalLabel, internalValue string, err error)\\n89: \\n90: // NewScheme creates a new Scheme. This scheme is pluggable by default.\\n91: func NewScheme() *Scheme {\\n92: \\ts := &Scheme{\\n93: \\t\\tgvkToType:                 map[schema.GroupVersionKind]reflect.Type{},\\n94: \\t\\ttypeToGVK:                 map[reflect.Type][]schema.GroupVersionKind{},\\n95: \\t\\tunversionedTypes:          map[reflect.Type]schema.GroupVersionKind{},\\n96: \\t\\tunversionedKinds:          map[string]reflect.Type{},\\n97: \\t\\tfieldLabelConversionFuncs: map[schema.GroupVersionKind]FieldLabelConversionFunc{},\\n98: \\t\\tdefaulterFuncs:            map[reflect.Type]func(interface{}){},\\n99: \\t\\tversionPriority:           map[string][]string{},\\n100: \\t\\tschemeName:                naming.GetNameFromCallsite(internalPackages...),\\n101: \\t}\\n102: \\ts.converter = conversion.NewConverter(nil)\\n103: \\n104: \\t// Enable couple default conversions by default.\\n105: \\tutilruntime.Must(RegisterEmbeddedConversions(s))\\n106: \\tutilruntime.Must(RegisterStringConversions(s))\\n107: \\treturn s\\n108: }\\n109: \\n110: // Converter allows access to the converter for the scheme\\n111: func (s *Scheme) Converter() *conversion.Converter {\\n112: \\treturn s.converter\\n113: }\\n114: \\n115: // AddUnversionedTypes registers the provided types as \\\"unversioned\\\", which means that they follow special rules.\\n116: // Whenever an object of this type is serialized, it is serialized with the provided group version and is not\\n117: // converted. Thus unversioned objects are expected to remain backwards compatible forever, as if they were in an\\n118: // API group and version that would never be updated.\\n119: //\\n120: // TODO: there is discussion about removing unversioned and replacing it with objects that are manifest into\\n121: // every version with particular schemas. Resolve this method at that point.\\n122: func (s *Scheme) AddUnversionedTypes(version schema.GroupVersion, types ...Object) {\\n123: \\ts.addObservedVersion(version)\\n124: \\ts.AddKnownTypes(version, types...)\\n125: \\tfor _, obj := range types {\\n126: \\t\\tt := reflect.TypeOf(obj).Elem()\\n127: \\t\\tgvk := version.WithKind(t.Name())\\n128: \\t\\ts.unversionedTypes[t] = gvk\\n129: \\t\\tif old, ok := s.unversionedKinds[gvk.Kind]; ok && t != old {\\n130: \\t\\t\\tpanic(fmt.Sprintf(\\\"%v.%v has already been registered as unversioned kind %q - kind name must be unique in scheme %q\\\", old.PkgPath(), old.Name(), gvk, s.schemeName))\\n131: \\t\\t}\\n132: \\t\\ts.unversionedKinds[gvk.Kind] = t\\n133: \\t}\\n134: }\\n135: \\n136: // AddKnownTypes registers all types passed in 'types' as being members of version 'version'.\\n137: // All objects passed to types should be pointers to structs. The name that go reports for\\n138: // the struct becomes the \\\"kind\\\" field when encoding. Version may not be empty - use the\\n139: // APIVersionInternal constant if you have a type that does not have a formal version.\\n140: func (s *Scheme) AddKnownTypes(gv schema.GroupVersion, types ...Object) {\\n141: \\ts.addObservedVersion(gv)\\n142: \\tfor _, obj := range types {\\n143: \\t\\tt := reflect.TypeOf(obj)\\n144: \\t\\tif t.Kind() != reflect.Pointer {\\n145: \\t\\t\\tpanic(\\\"All A scheme is the\\n34: // foundation for a versioned API and versioned configuration over time.\\n35: //\\n36: // In a Scheme, a Type is a particular Go struct, a Version is a point-in-time\\n37: // identifier for a particular representation of that Type (typically backwards\\n38: // compatible), a Kind is the unique name for that Type within the Version, and a\\n39: // Group identifies a set of Versions, Kinds, and Types that evolve over time. An\\n40: // Unversioned Type is one that is not yet formally bound to a type and is promised\\n41: // to be backwards compatible (effectively a \\\"v1\\\" of a Type that does not expect\\n42: // to break in the future).\\n43: //\\n44: // Schemes are not expected to change at runtime and are only threadsafe after\\n45: // registration is complete.\\n46: type Scheme struct {\\n47: \\t// gvkToType allows one to figure out the go type of an object with\\n48: \\t// the given version and name.\\n49: \\tgvkToType map[schema.GroupVersionKind]reflect.Type\\n50: \\n51: \\t// typeToGVK allows one to find metadata for a given go object.\\n52: \\t// The reflect.Type we index by should *not* be a pointer.\\n53: \\ttypeToGVK map[reflect.Type][]schema.GroupVersionKind\\n54: \\n55: \\t// unversionedTypes are transformed without conversion in ConvertToVersion.\\n56: \\tunversionedTypes map[reflect.Type]schema.GroupVersionKind\\n57: \\n58: \\t// unversionedKinds are the names of kinds that can be created in the context of any group\\n59: \\t// or version\\n60: \\t// TODO: resolve the status of unversioned types.\\n61: \\tunversionedKinds map[string]reflect.Type\\n62: \\n63: \\t// Map from version and resource to the corresponding func to convert\\n64: \\t// resource field labels in that version to internal version.\\n65: \\tfieldLabelConversionFuncs map[schema.GroupVersionKind]FieldLabelConversionFunc\\n66: \\n67: \\t// defaulterFuncs is a map to funcs to be called with an object to provide defaulting\\n68: \\t// the provided object must be a pointer.\\n69: \\tdefaulterFuncs map[reflect.Type]func(interface{})\\n70: \\n71: \\t// converter stores all registered conversion functions. It doesn't use a GroupVersion to avoid custom marshalling\n96: type GroupVersionResource struct {\n97: \tGroup    string\n98: \tVersion  string\n99: \tResource string\n100: }\n101: \n102: func (gvr GroupVersionResource) Empty() bool {\n103: \treturn len(gvr.Group) == 0 && len(gvr.Version) == 0 && len(gvr.Resource) == 0\n104: }\n105: \n106: func (gvr GroupVersionResource) GroupResource() GroupResource {\n107: \treturn GroupResource{Group: gvr.Group, Resource: gvr.Resource}\n108: }\n109: \n110: func (gvr GroupVersionResource) GroupVersion() GroupVersion {\n111: \treturn GroupVersion{Group: gvr.Group, Version: gvr.Version}\n112: }\n113: \n114: func (gvr GroupVersionResource) String() string {\n115: \treturn strings.Join([]string{gvr.Group, \"/\", gvr.Version, \", Resource=\", gvr.Resource}, \"\")\n116: }\n117: \n118: // GroupKind specifies a Group and a Kind, but does not force a version. The host might be resolved via external\n120: \t// DNS in some apiservers (e.g., `kube-apiserver` cannot resolve\n121: \t// in-cluster DNS as that would be a layering violation). `host` may\n122: \t// also be an IP address.\n123: \t//\n124: \t// Please note that using `localhost` or `127.0.0.1` as a `host` is\n125: \t// risky unless you take great care to run this webhook on all hosts\n126: \t// which run an apiserver which might need to make calls to this\n127: \t// webhook. `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/register.go` — Scheme registration for CRD types (GVK→Go type mapping)\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/install/` — Installation functions for registering CRD types into schemes\n\n### Server-Side Storage & Validation (apiextensions-apiserver)\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/registry/customresource/etcd.go` — CustomResourceStorage: generic etcd backend using Unstructured\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/registry/customresource/strategy.go` — Storage strategy for create/update/delete operations\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/validation/` — Schema validation using OpenAPI/JSONSchema\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/customresource_handler.go` — HTTP handler: routes API requests to storage layer (lines 86-100 show crdHandler routing)\n\n### Client-Side Access (client-go)\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/dynamic/simple.go` — DynamicClient: generic REST client for any GVR, works with Unstructured\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/dynamic/dynamicinformer/informer.go` — DynamicSharedInformerFactory & dynamicInformer: watches and caches Unstructured objects\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/dynamic/dynamiclister/lister.go` — dynamicLister: queries local cache using indexer\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/informers/factory.go` — SharedInformerFactory: base factory for typed informers (similar pattern)\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/tools/cache/` — SharedIndexInformer: watch→cache→indexer foundation\n\n---\n\n## Dependency Chain\n\n### 1. Foundation: apimachinery Types (Everything Depends On This)\n\n**Core Types:**\n- **TypeMeta** (`runtime/types.go`): Holds `apiVersion` and `kind` strings for all API objects\n- **Scheme** (`runtime/scheme.go`): Central type registry\n  - Maps `GroupVersionKind` ↔ Go types (e.g., `apiextensions.k8s.io/v1.CustomResourceDefinition` ↔ `*apiextensionsv1.CustomResourceDefinition`)\n  - Maps `reflect.Type` ↔ `GroupVersionKind` (reverse lookup)\n  - Manages conversion and defaulting functions\n- **GroupVersionKind / GroupVersionResource** (`runtime/schema/group_version.go`):\n  - **GVK** = `(Group, Version, Kind)` — identifies a type\n  - **GVR** = `(Group, Version, Resource)` — identifies a REST endpoint\n  - Conversion methods: `gvk.GroupVersion()`, `gvr.GroupResource()`, etc.\n- **Unstructured** (`apis/meta/v1/unstructured/unstructured.go`):\n  - Generic object: `Object map[string]interface{}`\n  - Implements `runtime.Object` interface (has GVK/ObjectMeta)\n  - Enables working with types without Go structs (critical for CRDs)\n\n---\n\n### 2. Type Definitions: CRD Types (apiextensions-apiserver)\n\n**Two-Version Pattern:**\n- **Internal Hub** (`pkg/apis/apiextensions/types.go`):\n  - `CustomResourceDefinition` struct with `TypeMeta`, `ObjectMeta`, `Spec`, `Status`\n  - Hub version for conversion (never exposed on wire)\n  - Registered in internal scheme via `register.go:addKnownTypes()`\n\n- **External v1** (`pkg/apis/apiextensions/v1/types.go`):\n  - Public `CustomResourceDefinition` struct (mirrors internal structure)\n  - Exposed on wire as `apiextensions.k8s.io/v1`\n  - Conversion functions between internal ↔ v1 registered in scheme\n\n**Scheme Registration** (`register.go`):\n```go\nSchemeGroupVersion = schema.GroupVersion{Group: \"apiextensions.k8s.io\", Version: runtime.APIVersionInternal}\nSchemeBuilder.AddToScheme() // Registers CRD types in scheme\n```\nThis allows the Scheme to:\n1. Decode `apiextensions.k8s.io/v1.CustomResourceDefinition` YAML/JSON → internal Hub struct → Go object\n2. Encode Go objects → internal Hub struct → wire format\n3. Convert between versions if multiple exist\n\n---\n\n### 3. Server-Side Lifecycle: Request → Validation → Storage → Etcd\n\n**HTTP Handler Entry Point** (`customresource_handler.go`):\n```go\ntype crdHandler struct {\n    versionDiscoveryHandler *versionDiscoveryHandler\n    groupDiscoveryHandler   *groupDiscoveryHandler\n    customStorageLock       sync.Mutex\n    customStorage           atomic.Value  // crdStorageMap\n    crdLister               listers.CustomResourceDefinitionLister\n    delegate                http.Handler\n    restOptionsGetter       generic.RESTOptionsGetter\n}\n```\n- Acts as filter for `/apis` endpoint\n- Routes requests to custom resource handlers based on GVR\n\n**Validation** (`apiserver/validation/`):\n- OpenAPI schema validation using JSONSchema\n- Structural pruning: removes fields not in CRD spec\n- Managed fields tracking\n\n**Storage Layer** (`registry/customresource/etcd.go`):\n```go\ntype CustomResourceStorage struct {\n    CustomResource *REST\n    Status         *StatusREST\n    Scale          *ScaleREST\n}\n\n// NewStorage creates generic registry.Store with Unstructured\nstore := &genericregistry.Store{\n    NewFunc: func() runtime.Object {\n        ret := &unstructured.Unstructured{}\n        ret.SetGroupVersionKind(kind)\n        return ret\n    },\n    CreateStrategy: strategy,\n    UpdateStrategy: strategy,\n    DeleteStrategy: strategy,\n}\n```\n- Uses `unstructured.Unstructured` for all CRD instances\n- No Go struct needed—Unstructured is \"structurally typed\" via JSONPath\n- Etcd stores JSON; Unstructured wraps it in `map[string]interface{}`\n- Strategies handle validation, conflict detection, field updates\n\n**Serialization Bridge:**\n- TypeMeta + ObjectMeta embedded in Unstructured.Object map\n- When stored: `Unstructured` → JSON → etcd\n- When fetched: etcd JSON → `Unstructured` → REST response\n\n---\n\n### 4. Client-Side Lifecycle: Discovery → Watch → Cache → Lister\n\n**Dynamic Client** (`dynamic/simple.go`):\n```go\ntype DynamicClient struct {\n    client rest.Interface\n}\n\nfunc (c *dynamicResourceClient) Create(ctx context.Context,\n    obj *unstructured.Unstructured, ...) (*unstructured.Unstructured, error)\n```\n- Takes `schema.GroupVersionResource` → constructs URL path\n- Works with `unstructured.Unstructured` (no typed client)\n- REST operations: Get, List, Watch, Create, Update, Delete, Patch\n- Handles `Unstructured` ↔ JSON encoding/decoding\n\n**Informer (Watch & Cache)** (`dynamic/dynamicinformer/informer.go`):\n```go\ntype DynamicSharedInformerFactory interface {\n    ForResource(gvr schema.GroupVersionResource) informers.GenericInformer\n}\n\ntype dynamicSharedInformerFactory struct {\n    client        dynamic.Interface\n    informers     map[schema.GroupVersionResource]informers.GenericInformer\n    startedInformers map[schema.GroupVersionResource]bool\n}\n\n// NewFilteredDynamicInformer constructs informer using:\ncache.NewSharedIndexInformerWithOptions(\n    client.Resource(gvr).Watch(...),  // Uses DynamicClient to watch\n    cache.Indexers{cache.NamespaceIndex: cache.MetaNamespaceIndexFunc},\n)\n```\n- Factory creates informers per GVR\n- Each informer watches API server: `client.Resource(gvr).Watch()`\n- Updates go to `SharedIndexInformer` → local cache (in-memory)\n- Indexer allows fast lookups: by namespace, by name, custom predicates\n\n**Lister (Cache Query)** (`dynamic/dynamiclister/lister.go`):\n```go\ntype dynamicLister struct {\n    indexer cache.Indexer\n    gvr     schema.GroupVersionResource\n}\n\nfunc (l *dynamicLister) List(selector labels.Selector) ([]*unstructured.Unstructured, error) {\n    cache.ListAll(l.indexer, selector, func(m interface{}) {\n        ret = append(ret, m.(*unstructured.Unstructured))\n    })\n}\n\nfunc (l *dynamicLister) Get(name string) (*unstructured.Unstructured, error) {\n    obj, exists, err := l.indexer.GetByKey(name)  // O(1) local lookup\n    return obj.(*unstructured.Unstructured), nil\n}\n```\n- Queries the in-memory indexer (no API calls)\n- Returns `Unstructured` for any GVR\n- Namespace-scoped and cluster-scoped aware\n\n---\n\n## Architectural Analysis\n\n### Cross-Project Integration\n\n**How the Four Projects Work Together:**\n\n1. **apimachinery** provides the protocol:\n   - All K8s objects inherit TypeMeta/ObjectMeta (metadata protocol)\n   - Scheme is the central type registry\n   - GVK/GVR are the coordinate system\n   - Unstructured enables \"schema-free\" objects\n\n2. **apiextensions-apiserver** uses apimachinery to define CRD type itself:\n   - CustomResourceDefinition is just another Kubernetes object (uses TypeMeta, ObjectMeta)\n   - Registered in Scheme like any other type\n   - BUT: the *instances* of a CRD (what users create) are stored as Unstructured\n\n3. **apiextensions-apiserver** storage layer:\n   - HTTP handler receives requests for CRD instances\n   - Validation: JSON schema check against CRD spec\n   - Storage: wraps instance JSON in Unstructured, stores in etcd\n   - Response: Unstructured → JSON → client\n\n4. **client-go** provides generic access:\n   - DynamicClient: Takes GVR, sends REST requests (no code generation)\n   - DynamicInformer: Watches any GVR via DynamicClient, caches as Unstructured\n   - DynamicLister: Queries cache (same pattern as typed listers)\n\n### The Scheme: Binding Layer\n\nThe **Scheme** is the critical checkpoint between server and client:\n\n**Server side:**\n- Scheme decodes incoming YAML/JSON using GVK information\n- If type is registered (built-in like Pod) → uses Go struct\n- If type is NOT registered (CRD instance) → falls through to Unstructured\n- Unstructured validation happens in apiextensions handler, not Scheme\n\n**Client side:**\n- Typed client: generated code uses Scheme to decode responses → typed structs\n- Dynamic client: Scheme not used; decoding is hardcoded to Unstructured via `unstructured.UnstructuredJSONScheme`\n\n### Why Unstructured is the CRD Solution\n\n**Problem:** CRDs are user-defined; server can't pre-generate Go structs\n**Solution:** Unstructured = `map[string]interface{}`\n- No struct needed; purely schema-free\n- Implements `runtime.Object` → can be stored, serialized, cached\n- Schema validation happens in apiextensions handler, not codec layer\n- Works with any tool that speaks the K8s Object interface (informers, listers, etc.)\n\n### Data Flow: From Write to Read\n\n**Write Path (Client → etcd):**\n1. Client creates `Unstructured` object with `apiVersion`, `kind`, `metadata`, custom fields\n2. DynamicClient.Create() → encodes to JSON\n3. HTTP POST to `/apis/GROUP/VERSION/RESOURCE` (custom_resource_handler.go)\n4. crdHandler routes to customResourceDefinition-specific handler\n5. Validation: JSON schema check against CRD spec\n6. Storage strategy: Validation, conflict resolution, managed fields\n7. GenericStore wraps JSON in `Unstructured`, stores in etcd as JSON\n\n**Read Path (etcd → Client Informer):**\n1. Client creates DynamicSharedInformerFactory for a GVR\n2. Informer watches `client.Resource(gvr).Watch()`\n3. DynamicClient.Watch() → HTTP GET with ?watch=true\n4. Server streams events (ADDED, MODIFIED, DELETED)\n5. Informer receives events → caches each object as Unstructured\n6. Lister queries cache: O(1) by key, O(n) with label selector\n7. Application calls `lister.Get(name)` → returns Unstructured\n\n---\n\n## Cross-Project Dependency Visualization\n\n```\n                         apimachinery (Foundation)\n                         ├─ Scheme: GVK↔Type registry\n                         ├─ TypeMeta/ObjectMeta: metadata protocol\n                         ├─ GVK/GVR: coordinate system\n                         └─ Unstructured: schema-free object\n                                  ↑\n                    ┌─────────────┼─────────────┐\n                    ↓             ↓             ↓\n            apiextensions-apiserver   client-go    (api)\n             (Server/Storage)         (Client)     (Type defs)\n            ┌──────────────────┐    ┌──────────┐   ┌─────────┐\n            │ CRD Definition   │    │ Dynamic  │   │ Built-in│\n            │ (TypeMeta+Spec)  │    │ Client   │   │ Types   │\n            ├──────────────────┤    ├──────────┤   └─────────┘\n            │ HTTP Handler     │    │ Informer │\n            │ (customresource) │    │ (Watch+  │\n            ├──────────────────┤    │  Cache)  │\n            │ Validation       │    ├──────────┤\n            │ (JSON Schema)    │    │ Lister   │\n            ├──────────────────┤    │ (Query   │\n            │ Storage (etcd)   │←→→ │  Cache)  │\n            │ (Unstructured)   │    └──────────┘\n            └──────────────────┘\n```\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nThe CRD lifecycle is a masterpiece of separation of concerns:\n\n1. **apimachinery** provides the universal object model (TypeMeta, Scheme, GVK, Unstructured) that enables schema-independent type handling.\n\n2. **apiextensions-apiserver** implements the CRD concept: it stores CRD *definitions* (which are normal K8s objects) and uses their schemas to validate and store CRD *instances* as Unstructured JSON.\n\n3. **client-go** provides generic watch/cache/lister for any GVR via the Dynamic client family, reusing the same informer/lister patterns as typed clients but with Unstructured.\n\n4. **api** holds built-in type definitions; CRDs extend this without code generation.\n\nThe checkpoint between server and client is the **Scheme and Unstructured**: on the server, validation is explicit (JSON schema in apiextensions); on the client, it's implicit (tools consume Unstructured generically). This enables users to define new resources at runtime without recompiling the apiserver—a key feature of Kubernetes extensibility.\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":10,"cache_creation_input_tokens":547,"cache_read_input_tokens":84091,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":547},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"441c4331-228d-4584-9b21-a9cedb15d911","uuid":"1ce16334-f6d1-49ac-9f5f-72eb3e737762"}

Storage strategy: Validation, conflict resolution, managed fields\n7. GenericStore wraps JSON in `Unstructured`, stores in etcd as JSON\n\n**Read Path (etcd → Client Informer):**\n1. Client creates DynamicSharedInformerFactory for a GVR\n2. Informer watches `client.Resource(gvr).Watch()`\n3. DynamicClient.Watch() → HTTP GET with ?watch=true\n4. Server streams events (ADDED, MODIFIED, DELETED)\n5. Informer receives events → caches each object as Unstructured\n6. Lister queries cache: O(1) by key, O(n) with label selector\n7. Application calls `lister.Get(name)` → returns Unstructured\n\n---\n\n## Cross-Project Dependency Visualization\n\n```\n                         apimachinery (Foundation)\n                         ├─ Scheme: GVK↔Type registry\n                         ├─ TypeMeta/ObjectMeta: metadata protocol\n                         ├─ GVK/GVR: coordinate system\n                         └─ Unstructured: schema-free object\n                                  ↑\n                    ┌─────────────┼─────────────┐\n                    ↓             ↓             ↓\n            apiextensions-apiserver   client-go    (api)\n             (Server/Storage)         (Client)     (Type defs)\n            ┌──────────────────┐    ┌──────────┐   ┌─────────┐\n            │ CRD Definition   │    │ Dynamic  │   │ Built-in│\n            │ (TypeMeta+Spec)  │    │ Client   │   │ Types   │\n            ├──────────────────┤    ├──────────┤   └─────────┘\n            │ HTTP Handler     │    │ Informer │\n            │ (customresource) │    │ (Watch+  │\n            ├──────────────────┤    │  Cache)  │\n            │ Validation       │    ├──────────┤\n            │ (JSON Schema)    │    │ Lister   │\n            ├──────────────────┤    │ (Query   │\n            │ Storage (etcd)   │←→→ │  Cache)  │\n            │ (Unstructured)   │    └──────────┘\n            └──────────────────┘\n```\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nThe CRD lifecycle is a masterpiece of separation of concerns:\n\n1. **apimachinery** provides the universal object model (TypeMeta, Scheme, GVK, Unstructured) that enables schema-independent type handling.\n\n2. **apiextensions-apiserver** implements the CRD concept: it stores CRD *definitions* (which are normal K8s objects) and uses their schemas to validate and store CRD *instances* as Unstructured JSON.\n\n3. **client-go** provides generic watch/cache/lister for any GVR via the Dynamic client family, reusing the same informer/lister patterns as typed clients but with Unstructured.\n\n4. **api** holds built-in type definitions; CRDs extend this without code generation.\n\nThe checkpoint between server and client is the **Scheme and Unstructured**: on the server, validation is explicit (JSON schema in apiextensions); on the client, it's implicit (tools consume Unstructured generically). This enables users to define new resources at runtime without recompiling the apiserver—a key feature of Kubernetes extensibility.\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
